ADDITIONAL NOTES
Headline references have been standardized according to the following pattern:
Bhvibh_n.n. = BhikkhuvibhaÇga_Class of offence(Roman).rule(Arabic).
BhnÅvibh_n.n. = BhikkhuïÅvibhaÇga_Class of offence(Roman).rule(Arabic).

to plain Roman type in the original Dhammakaya file.
